#  file: rfProjTopic2010-May.txt
#  package: rfRawData
#  description of file/package:
#
#  This package includes raw data files from our database of RubyForge project 
#  information generated from the list of projects gathered in 2010-May
#
#  Raw html data was inserted into database by running our java-based Rubyforge 
#  spidering program based on the libraries at ossmole.sf.net in our CVS tree.
#  This html data was then parsed and scraped to extract interesting facts.
#
#  Scripts & raw data available at http://flossmole.org
#  Scripts written by Megan Squire and contributed to the FLOSSmole project
#
#  This data is free and available for any use (after all we just spidered it ;)
#  We do however request that those using the data in any published form provide 
#  a citation to: FLOSSmole Project (2004-2010) 
#  The project is available at: http://flossmole.org
#

#  FROM rf_project_topic
#  WHERE datasource_id=219
#  ORDER BY proj_unixname
#
#  datasource_id = 219 is the 2010-May run on Rubyforge.
